#########################################################################
# 3183000 - 3183999	USSR events
#########################################################################

event = {
	id = 3183084 #Soviet AI gets IC bonus against human Germany => taken from events that trigger later normally
	random = no
	country = SOV
	
	trigger = {
				NOT = { local_flag = SOV_AI_IC }
				NOT = { AI = GER }
				AI = SOV
				}
	
	name = "AI_EVENT"
	# desc = "AI_EVENT"
	style = 0
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = january year = 1936 } #shall only trigger at the beginning in order to not confuse with later events

	action_a = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { type = peacetime_ic_mod value = 20 }
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = total value = 15 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = SOV_AI_IC }
		}
}

	picture = "Mol_Rib"

		name = ACTIONNAME3183000A # A Most Excellent Proposition
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = end_guarantee which = SOV where = FRA }
		command = { type = trigger which = 2013 }
		# Claims on Finland
		command = { type = addcore which = 530 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 531 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 532 }
		command = { type = relation which = GER value = 10 }
		command = { type = relation which = FIN value = -5 }
		command = { type = relation which = POL value = -5 }
		command = { type = relation which = LIT value = -5 }
		command = { type = relation which = LAT value = -5 }
		command = { type = relation which = EST value = -5 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 1 }
		command = { type = money value = 75 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = SOV_AI_IC } } type = industrial_modifier which = total value = 5 } #counters reduced starting efficiency
		command = { type = trade which = SOV where = GER oil = -20 supplies = 3 value = 1 } #tradeoff for IC
	}
	action_b = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3183000B # No deals with the enemies of the Workers!
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = trigger which = 3136024 }
		command = { type = relation which = GER value = -15 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = ACTIONNAME3183000C # Propose an unholy alliance
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = relation which = GER value = 15 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 2015 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { local_flag = SOV_AI_IC } } type = industrial_modifier which = total value = 5 } #counters reduced starting efficiency
		command = { type = trade which = SOV where = GER oil = -20 supplies = 3 value = 1 } #tradeoff for IC
	}
}

			}

			control = { province = 302 data = SOV } # Hotin, Bessarabia

#########################################################################
#  The Finnish Winter War (was 2620)
#########################################################################
event = { 
	id = 2620 # Referenced in AI files
	random = no
	country = SOV
	
	save_date = yes
	
	trigger = {
		exists = FIN
		NOT = {
			war = { country = GER country = SOV }
			alliance = { country = FIN country = GER }
			alliance = { country = FIN country = ENG }
			exists = POL
			OR = {
				war = { country = FIN country = SOV }
				war = { country = GER country = SOV }
				alliance = { country = FIN country = SOV }
				control = { province = 530 data = SOV }
				control = { province = 531 data = SOV }
				control = { province = 532 data = SOV }
				ispuppet = FIN
				ispuppet = SOV
			}
		}
		war = { country = GER country = ENG }
	}
	
	name = "EVT_2620_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_2620_DESC"
	style = 2
	picture = "finland_sweden"
	
	date = { day = 13 month = november year = 1939 }
	offset = 7
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1940 }
	
	action_a = {
		name = ACTIONNAME2620A # Press claims
		ai_chance = 99
		command = { type = relation which = FIN value = -10 }
		command = { type = relation which = SWE value = -5 }
		command = { type = relation which = NOR value = -5 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 3200 } # FIN

event = {
	id = 3183077
	random = no
	country = SOV
	
	save_date = yes
	
	trigger = {
				war = { country = GER country = SOV }
				}
	
	name = EVT_3183077_NAME
	desc = EVT_3183077_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "sov_red_army_recovery"
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action_a = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV } type = local_clrflag which = SOVBuildStandard }
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV } type = local_clrflag which = SOVBuildLand }
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV } type = local_setflag which = SOVBuildLandPanic }
		
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV NOT = { local_flag = activation_light_infantry }} type = ai which = "switch/SOV_Build_Panic.ai" }
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV local_flag = activation_light_infantry } type = ai which = "switch/SOV_Build_Panic_light.ai" }
		
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV not = { ai = GER } } type = tc_mod value = 200 } # gives soviet AI a TC bonus against a human GER
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV not = { ai = GER } } type = local_setflag which = SOV_AI_TC }
		
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV ai = GER } type = dissent value = 10 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV NOT = { ai = GER } } type = dissent value = -5 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { ai = SOV } NOT = { ai = GER } } type = dissent value = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { NOT = { ai = SOV } ai = GER } type = dissent value = 15 }
		
		command = { type = end_trades which = SOV where = GER }
		}
}

###########################################################################
# AI gets winter bonus on GDE
###########################################################################

event = {
	id = 3183085
	random = no
	country = SOV
	
	persistent = yes
	
	trigger = {
				event = 3183051 #winter equipment
				NOT = { local_flag = SOV_winter_GDE }
				NOT = { local_flag = SOV_winter_GDE_6690 }
				NOT = { local_flag = SOV_winter_GDE_AIAI }
				AI = SOV
				war = { country = GER country = SOV }
				month = 10 # at least November; 0 = january, 11 = december
				NOT = { month = 4 } # at latest April
	}
	
	name = AI_EVENT
	# desc = AI_EVENT
	style = 0
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action_a = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		
		# tech 6690 = last SOV land doctrine, raising GDE by 0.025
		
		# sets soviet GDE to a maximum of 0.82 after purge event effect has vanished
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV NOT = { ai = GER } NOT = { technology = { country = SOV value = 6690 } } } type = ground_def_eff value = 0.045 when = 1 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = SOV_winter_GDE }
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV NOT = { ai = GER } technology = { country = SOV value = 6690 } } type = ground_def_eff value = 0.02 when = 1 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = SOV_winter_GDE_6690 }
		
		# sets soviet GDE to a maximum of 0.80 after purge event effect has vanished
		command = { trigger = { ai = SOV ai = GER NOT = { technology = { country = SOV value = 6690 } } } type = ground_def_eff value = 0.025 when = 1 }
		command = { type = local_setflag which = SOV_winter_GDE_AIAI }
		
	}
}
	
###########################################################################
# AI winter bonus on GDE removed
###########################################################################

event = {
	id = 3183086
	random = no
	country = SOV
	
	persistent = yes
	
	trigger = {
				OR = {
						local_flag = SOV_winter_GDE
						local_flag = SOV_winter_GDE_6690
						local_flag = SOV_winter_GDE_AIAI
						}
				OR = {
						NOT = { AI = SOV }
						NOT = { war = { country = GER country = SOV } }
						month = 4 # at least May
						}
				NOT = { month = 10 } # at latest October
	}
	
	name = AI_EVENT
	# desc = AI_EVENT
	style = 0
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1936 }
	offset = 1
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1999 }

	action_a = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		
		# tech 6690 = last SOV land doctrine, raising GDE by 0.025
		
		# sets soviet GDE to a maximum of 0.82 after purge event effect has vanished
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = SOV_winter_GDE } 		type = ground_def_eff value = -0.045 when = 1 }
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = SOV_winter_GDE_6690 } 	type = ground_def_eff value = -0.02 when = 1 }
		
		# sets soviet GDE to a maximum of 0.80 after purge event effect has vanished
		command = { trigger = { local_flag = SOV_winter_GDE_AIAI } 	type = ground_def_eff value = -0.025 when = 1 }
		
		command = { type = local_setflag which = SOV_winter_GDE }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 3183010
	random = no
	country = SOV
	
	trigger = {
				OR = {
						control = { province = 55 data = GER } # Paris is in German hands
						NOT = { exists = GER } # backup trigger 1
						war = { country = GER country = SOV } # backup trigger 2
						}
				OR = {
						event = 3183089
						event = 3183091
						event = 3183093
						}
				OR = {
						exists = LIT
						exists = LAT
						exists = EST
						}			
	}
	
	name = EVT_3183010_NAME
	desc = EVT_3183010_DESC
	style = 2
	picture = "sov_event_baltics_end" #"sov_baltics_end"

	offset = 1

		command = { type = addcore which = 268 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 269 }

		command = { type = addcore which = 273 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 272 }

		command = { type = addcore which = 275 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 274 }
		command = { type = addcore which = 270 }
#		command = { type = trigger which = 3132001 }
		command = { type = money value = 95 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 1 }
